< review>
I came here for dinner with 15 of our family members as soon as they opened back up (covid) because my Uncle always says how good they are.
I'm not a big sushi eater, maybe once or twice a year. But this is the best sushi restaurant I've been to. We had the avocado rolls, 911 rolls, spicy tuna with avocado, bsc rolls, spicy edamame,  yellowtail, and blue fin. Wow, it was all amazing. I have never eaten this much sushi, but I couldn't stop.

The sushi, in my opinion, is pretty good. My kids and I love going here and getting the food.  The restaurant is pretty clean but a little chaotic. The chefs behind the bar are very friendly and knowledgeable about the food. But the waiting staff is some of the worst in santa Clarita. They do not answer the phone so good luck ordering take out.  There is one older woman who knows what she is doing but if you get one of the younger girls, good luck.  A visit could last hours while you never get any attention or even sometimes the right order. But the food is good enough that we endure it anyway. If you have the time to think ahead driving over and ordering to go and then going grocery shopping at the Albertsons near by and then picking it up on the way out is probably your best bet.</text>

<user>106908841677725720888<//user><name>L F</name><time>1571871915661<//time><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
This place is a family favorite. It's always been great and delicious.  We've tried a variety of dishes and they're all wonderful. Two things set this sushi restaurant apart from others:
1. You don't just have to rely on just soy sauce, they have delicious sauces that bring out the flavor of the rolls, without overwhelming it such as ponzu yuzu, eel sauce, spicy or sweet mayo, etc.
2. Their non-spicy sushi rolls are actually not spicy.  I've come across spicy items (wasabi or a dash of sriracha) mixed into non spicy rolls far too often at other sushi restaurants. Their regular spicy rolls are also not overwhelming.< /review>

Good place to make your own copies and print documents. You can email your documents to "printandgo@fedex.com" then print them at the store with a code sent to your email. You get a card at the store and add cash to it or use your credit card. PAY ATTENTION OR YOU LOSE MONEY: the copy machines are set to COLOR Copies! You must change your choice to BLACK & WHITE! If you don't, you pay for color, which is expensive. Not sure why the default choice is color. I would give 5 stars on the copying if this was corrected.</text>

Made a quick stop to send off some goods. This Fedex is located in a super busy part of town right off of the 405 freeway Hawthorne exit.

Here's what liked...
* The location is convenient being right off of the freeway. However accessing the lot can be difficult.
* Love the customer service. The ladies at the front register were super friendly and helpful! I was caught off guard by the genuine smile and quick service :-)
* The parking lot for 8:30 am was excellent.
* There are plenty of places to eat in the plaza if you need a one-stop-shop location.

Here's what I didn't like...
* Accessing plaza was difficult with the rush hour traffic.<//Review>< pics>

Pretty cool little area. Bathrooms- yep, easy to spot, definitely not the hardest area in the world to hit, but a fun few hours especially if you're cool just picking a road and rolling. Room for Jeeps, sidebysides, OHV (according to regs) and my Tacoma made easy work of it, but there's quite a few spots where a full size would catch some pretty intense pinstriping! (Avoid Squints Farm area!) Probably a pretty cool area if it catches some snow! I'll be back soon.</text>

5<//Rate>
< text>
Took a fairly stock jeep lj up there and it handled the trails fine. Be prepared to air down a bit because there are sections with small rocks throughout, nothing major though. There is a short decent right before going down to deep creek that I would recommend you have a decent lift and tires due to the size of the rocks if you want to make it down and park right next to the creek. We ran into a mixture of atvs, can-ams, dirt bikes, and offroad vehicles using the trails so be mindful, everyone was courteous though. Overall it is a great spot with a lot of trail variety.< /text>

< Review>
Me and my boyfriend stumbled upon this place while driving. He was hungry and was like lets try that place. Im a taco shop connoisseur, so I was like, NO, im not gonna go to a random tacoshop. He was like all good taco shops start with a P, its good trust. ( I dont know where his logic comes from). So maybe 3 days later. He's like I want Birria tacos. So we were headed to Birria Kings, then he was like lets try that taco shop we saw. Im side eyeing him, and was like i dont remember the name. He was like google maps it. So i did and found the name. We searched the instagram and it looked BOMB. So we went on my lunch we got the surf and turf burrito and 2 birria tacos. When i say it was SOOOOO good. I was mad we didn't go the first time we saw it. We ended up going the next day just for tacos and the Nachos it was just as good. In this corner, weighting in as the "cleanest" shop on El cajon blvd, I give you the Challenger Penelopes Mexican food.  I the vegetarian found the menu a little typical at first. Large lot right across the street from the go lounge and from what I've seen better food than chelatos and open more as well.  I wanna see what there menu looks like after the horde of la Mesa taste buds require.  Customer service on point. < Text>
Fast, courteous, professional.

I came into Golden Gate on Lombard mid-afternoon with a 2.5" long gash on my shin. I knew I would need stitches. The two receptionists greeted me promptly and courteously, and I signed in as a walk-in. Immediately, a screen displayed my approximate wait time. On this particular afternoon, I only had to wait 5-10 minutes before being called back to a room. The nurses on staff were kind, caring, and professional; and the nurse practitioner who stitched me up was really wonderful (Brandon, or Brendan). He was upbeat and communicative, and let me know what was happening every step of the way. He was careful in administering enough numbing medication so I wouldn't feel a thing, and he did a great job putting in 9 stitches and offering me all of the information I needed for follow-up care. Part of my good experience had to do with how quickly I was seen. This is, of course, highly variable, but the staff will post your wait time and take good care of you once it's your turn.< /Text>

I love trying out different branches for Noodles and co, this branch did not disappoint, we arrived around lunch time, the restaurant was nearly empty with only 2 tables occupied, when trying to decide with what to go with, the cashier lady was extremely friendly and helpful in suggesting a few, we ended up with spaghetti Alfredo ( omit the chicken), Mac & cheese for the kids, spicy green shrimp Thai curry(the new bowl that has been recently added to the menu) and garlic bread as a side dish, i really liked the taste of the Alfredo, not too much cheese and sauce that would be too empowering, my hubby on the other hand didn't like the new bowl, the combination between the pineapple, shrimps and sauce just didn't blend well, I'm afraid he would not be coming back to try Noodles and co as a result ,  as for me well lets just say ill have to come solo  from now on<//Review>
